          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class="date-header"><span>sábado, 4 de junio de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="5490928400359463042" itemprop="postId">
<a name="5490928400359463042"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/06/cambiar-tamano-de-disco-en-qemu-kvm.html">Cambiar tamaño de disco en qemu kvm</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5490928400359463042" itemprop="description articleBody">
Una posible forma es la siguiente, suponemos que el disco inicial es inicial.qcow2:<br><br>1.- crear disco de destino del tamaño deseado p.e. 60G<br>qemu-img create -f qcow2 destino.qcow2 60G<br><br>2.- arrancamos gparted con un sistema con los dos discos<br>qemu -hda inicial.qcow2 -hdb destino.qcow2 -cdrom=gparted.iso -boot d<br><br>3.- con el gparted hacemos copiar/pegar de un disco a otro con el nuevo tamaño deseado<br>(tarda bastante si los discos son grandes)<br><br>4.- comprobamos que boota y nuevo tamaño de disco<br>qemu -had destino.qcow2<br>hacemos df -h para comprobar nuevo tamaño<br><br>Si el nuevo dominio no arranca podemos usar la distribuición rescatux y regrabar el grub en la MBR (gràcies Victor ;-))<br><br>qemu -hda destino.qcow2 -cdron=rescatux.iso -boot d
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-footer">

<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="8896025386559385912" itemprop="postId">
<a name="8896025386559385912"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/06/pasar-de-virtualbox-kvm-o-xen.html">Pasar de VirtualBox a KVM o Xen</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8896025386559385912" itemprop="description articleBody">
Para pasar un disco de vdkm o vdi a qcow2 pasamos primero por raw. Es decir:<br><br>convertim vmdk de virtual box a raw:<br>VBoxManage internalcommands converttoraw aaa.vmdk file.raw<br><br>comprbar que boota<br>qemu -had file.raw<br><br>Convertimos raw a qcow2<br>qemu-img convert file.raw -O qcow2 imatge.qcow2<br><br>comprobar que boota<br>qemu -had imatge.qcow2
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-footer">

<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/06/como-virtualizar-con-ubuntu-kvm-y-no.html">Cómo virtualizar con ubuntu kvm y no morir en el intento</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-701702497379120273" itemprop="description articleBody">
Ni se os ocurra seguir la server guide porque no solo no funciona sino que confunde. El manual apropiado es el "community" <br><br><a href="https://help.ubuntu.com/community/KVM/Installation">Community KVM installation</a>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="961951226416942687" itemprop="postId">
<a name="961951226416942687"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/05/python-mas-aritmetica-con-meses.html">Python, más aritmética con meses</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-961951226416942687" itemprop="description articleBody">
<code><br>def suma_mes(current_date, month_step):<br>        """ suma month_setp mesos a current_date """<br>        carry, new_month=divmod(current_date.month-1+month_step, 12)<br>        new_month+=1<br>        return current_date.replace(year=current_date.year+carry, month=new_month)<br></code><br><br>¿Cuántos días faltan para el mismo día de hoy del mes que viene?<br><br><code><br>&gt;&gt;&gt; print (suma_mes(datetime.date.today(), 1)-datetime.date.today()).days<br></code>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="1982484138068914930" itemprop="postId">
<a name="1982484138068914930"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/05/sumar-un-mes-con-python.html">Sumar un mes con python</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1982484138068914930" itemprop="description articleBody">
<code><br>&gt;&gt;&gt; from datetime import date<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; current_date=date.today()<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; carry, new_month=divmod(current_date.month-1+1, 12)<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; new_month+=1<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; current_date=current_date.replace(year=current_date.year+carry, month=new_month)<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; print date.today()<br>2011-05-21<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; print current_date<br>2011-06-21<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; <br></code>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

<h2 class="date-header"><span>lunes, 4 de abril de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="5586384458339010033" itemprop="postId">
<a name="5586384458339010033"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/04/ubuntu-one-trabaja-con-iss.html">Ubuntu One trabaja con IIS!!!</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5586384458339010033" itemprop="description articleBody">
Anda que... estaba yo sicronizando música con Ubuntu One, me da un error de red y me sale:<div><br></div><div><span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: verdana; font-size: 11px; line-height: 16px; -webkit-border-horizontal-spacing: 10px; -webkit-border-vertical-spacing: 10px; "><h1 style="font: normal normal normal 13pt/15pt verdana; ">The page cannot be found</h1>The page you are looking for might have been removed, had its name changed, or is temporarily unavailable.<hr><p>Please try the following:</p><ul><li>Make sure that the Web site address displayed in the address bar of your browser is spelled and formatted correctly.</li><li>If you reached this page by clicking a link, contact the Web site administrator to alert them that the link is incorrectly formatted.</li><li>Click the <a href="http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=9191328551308072706&amp;postID=5586384458339010033" style="color: red; ">Back</a> button to try another link.</li></ul><h2 style="font: normal normal normal 8pt/12pt verdana; ">HTTP Error 404 - File or directory not found.<br>Internet Information Services (IIS)</h2><hr><p>Technical Information (for support personnel)</p><ul><li>Go to <a href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=8180" style="color: red; ">Microsoft Product Support Services</a> and perform a title search for the words <b>HTTP</b> and <b>404</b>.</li><li>Open <b>IIS Help</b>, which is accessible in IIS Manager (inetmgr), and search for topics titled <b>Web Site Setup</b>, <b>Common Administrative Tasks</b>, and<b>About Custom Error Messages</b>.</li></ul><div>UArrrrrrgggg!!</div></span></div>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

<h2 class="date-header"><span>viernes, 11 de marzo de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="6076735820115786324" itemprop="postId">
<a name="6076735820115786324"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/03/django-evitar-error-en-el-administrador.html">Django: Evitar error en el administrador "decoding Unicode is not supported"</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6076735820115786324" itemprop="description articleBody">
Si, como es probable, os habéis encontrado con este error en el administrador cuando examináis modelos con caracteres utf-8, creo que puede deberse al hecho de que django sirve los strings en unicode pero sin codificar.<br><br>En python, en el momento que intentamos algo como esto:<br><code><br>&gt;&gt;&gt; unicode('pepe', 'utf-8')<br>u'pepe'<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; unicode(u'pepe', 'utf-8')<br><br>Traceback (most recent call last):<br>File "<stdin>", line 1, in <module><br>TypeError: decoding Unicode is not supported<br></module></stdin></code><br>Obtenemos el TypeError. En el admin de django, el error lo obtendremos siempre que grabemos caracteres &gt;255. Parece provenir del hecho de codificar el unicode en ascii en vez de utf-8 ¿?.<br><br>Si hacemos:<br><code><br>def __unicode__(self):<br>   return unicode(self.descripcion)<br></code><br><br>Obtendremos el error de decodificación ascii, pero si hacemos...<br><br><code><br>def __unicode__(self):<br>   return unicode(self.descripcion, 'utf-8')<br></code><br><br>...nos funcionará pero no podremos usar el admin para examinar el modelo porque nos genera el error anterior.<br><br>Tenemos dos posibilidades, aunque no las comprendo en profundidad:<br><br>Solución 1):<br><code><br>from django.utils.encoding import smart_unicode<br></code><br>En los modelos poner:<br><code><br>def __unicode__(self):<br>   return smart_unicode(("%s" % self.descripcion))<br></code><br><br>Solución 2) Llamado "método del literal"<br><code><br>def __unicode__(self):<br>   return (u"%s" % self.descripcion)<br></code><br><br>En todo caso es conveniente poner el setting<br><code><br>DEFAULT_CHARSET='utf-8'<br></code><br>que fuerza utf-8 a la hora de procesar y servir las plantillas.<br><br>Más info sobre este tema estaría bien. En mi caso uso mysql con utf-8 y ordenación spanish2, ubuntu 10.10 con utf-8 y apache forzado a servir utf-8.
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class="date-header"><span>jueves, 10 de marzo de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="2953339392842286224" itemprop="postId">
<a name="2953339392842286224"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/03/django-guardar-imagenes-o-blobs-desde.html">Django: Guardar imágenes (o blobs) desde la red</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2953339392842286224" itemprop="description articleBody">
Debido a las consultas amplío el post anterior para aclarar un poco el proceso suponiendo que bajamos las imágenes desde un servidor sFTP, sólo hay que cambiar los parámetros de pycurl para operar con http, https, etc...<br><br>Primero bajamos la imagen a memoria con algún gestor (pycurl por ejemplo o urllib) y guardarlo en un cStringIO:<br><br><code><br>import pycurl, cStringIO<br><br>buf = cStringIO.StringIO() <br>url=('ftps://%s:990/%s' % (ip, fichero))<br>privatekey = '/home/sss/.ssh/id_rsa'<br>options = {<br>  pycurl.USERPWD: 'xxxxx:xxxx',<br>  pycurl.SSLKEYPASSWD: 'adfasdfasdfas',<br>  pycurl.SSH_PRIVATE_KEYFILE: privatekey,<br>  pycurl.SSH_PUBLIC_KEYFILE: privatekey + '.pub',<br>  #pycurl.WRITEDATA: open('/dev/null', 'wb'),<br>  pycurl.VERBOSE: 1,<br>  pycurl.URL: url,<br>  pycurl.HEADER: 1,<br>  pycurl.NOBODY: 1,<br>  pycurl.WRITEFUNCTION: buf.write,<br>  pycurl.NOPROGRESS: 1,<br>  pycurl.SSL_VERIFYPEER: 0,<br>  pycurl.SSL_VERIFYHOST: 0,<br>}<br> <br>gestor = pycurl.Curl()<br>try:<br>for (k, v) in options.items():<br>  print k, v<br>  gestor.setopt(k, v)<br>except Exception, msg:<br>  logging.info('Error setopt %s' % msg)<br><br>gestor.perform()<br><br></code><br><br>Ahora ya tenemos la imagen en memoria (buf), vamos a grabarla (django la graba en disco y en la db solo se guarda el path), el único problema es que ImageField espera un campo file, pero lo solucionaremos con un workaround:<br><br>En tu modelo pones:<br><code><br>class Persona(models.Model):<br> .....<br> imagen=models.ImageField(upload_to=settings.PATH_FOTOS_CLIENTES, blank=True)<br></code><br><br>Donde settings.PATH_FOTOS_CLIENTES apunta a la ruta que cuelga de la ruta que tengas en settings.MEDIA_ROOT y tiene el formato siguiente o similar (en settings.py):<br><br><code><br>PATH_FOTOS_CLIENTES='clientes/%Y/%m/%d'<br></code><br><br>Ahora tenemos que pasar de la imagen que tienes cargada en memoria a un stream tipo 'file' para que pueda ser guardado por el modelo:<br><br><code><br>from django.core.files.uploadedfile import SimpleUploadedFile<br><br>foto = SimpleUploadedFile('imagencliente.jpg',<br>         buf.getvalue(),<br>         "image/jpeg")<br></code><br><br>y ya salvamos:<br><code><br>p=Persona( imagen=foto )<br>p.save()<br></code><br><br>Comentad si os surge alguna duda.<br>Saludos,<br>Pere Vilás.
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class="date-header"><span>miércoles, 9 de marzo de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="4842941822219677402" itemprop="postId">
<a name="4842941822219677402"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/03/django-guardar-imagenes-desde-string.html">Django: Guardar imágenes desde string</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-4842941822219677402" itemprop="description articleBody">
Para guardar una imagen en un campo de tipo ImageField de Model desde una cadena como un POST http o desde memoria hacemos lo siguiente:<br><br><code><br>from django.core.files.uploadedfile import SimpleUploadedFile<br>import cStringIO<br><br>buf = cStringIO.StringIO()     <br># adquirimos imagen y la guardamos en buf i.e. mediante pycurl<br><br>foto = SimpleUploadedFile('imagen.jpg', buf.getvalue(), "image/jpeg")  <br><br># ahora foto contiene el stream pero en formato 'fichero'<br><br>p=Modelo( imagen=foto )<br>p.save()<br></code><br><br><br>Espero que os sirva ;-)
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-footer">
<div class="post-footer-line post-footer-line-1"><span class="post-author vcard">

<span class="fn" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
<meta content="https://plus.google.com/104068316018808569946" itemprop="url">
<a class="g-profile" href="https://plus.google.com/104068316018808569946" rel="author" title="author profile" data-gapiscan="true" data-onload="true" data-gapiattached="true">
<span itemprop="name">Pere Vilas</span>
</a>
</span>
</span>
<span class="post-timestamp">

<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="3701321002569746607" itemprop="postId">
<a name="3701321002569746607"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/03/django-en-la-red-con-el-servidor-de.html">Django en la red con el servidor de desarrollo</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3701321002569746607" itemprop="description articleBody">
No basta con python manage.py runserver [num_puerto], esto sólo lo hace accesible desde loopback, para servir en red hay que hacer<br><code><br>python manage.py runserver [ip_fisica]:[num_puerto]<br></code><br><br>Para saber nuestra ip podemos hacerlo con ifconfig, evidentemente no podemos usar localhost o 127.0.0.1
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class="date-header"><span>jueves, 24 de febrero de 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class="post-outer">
<div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
<meta content="9191328551308072706" itemprop="blogId">
<meta content="7208246413595847923" itemprop="postId">
<a name="7208246413595847923"></a>
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
<a href="http://www.pvilas.com/2011/02/consultas-en-django.html">Consultas en Django</a>
</h3>
<div class="post-header">
<div class="post-header-line-1"></div>
</div>
<div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7208246413595847923" itemprop="description articleBody">
<div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; "><h1 id="internal-source-marker_0.23160702199675143" style="font-size: medium; "><span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial; font-size: 15px; white-space: pre-wrap; font-weight: normal; ">Unos pequeños apuntes cogidos al vuelo de consultas en django</span></h1><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Un queryset sería el equivalente a un SELECT</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Un filter sería el equivalente a un WHERE</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Comandos de Query:</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Objeto.objects.all() -&gt; Todo el conjunto</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Objeto.objects.filter() -&gt; Un filtro para incluir</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Objeto.objects.exclude() -&gt; Un filtro para excluir</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Objeto.objects.get() -&gt; Busca un solo objeto</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Encadenado de filtros</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.filter(</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; "><span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre; "> </span>headline__startswith=’What’</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">).exclude(</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; "><span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre; "> </span>pub_date__gte=datetime.now()</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">).filter(</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; "><span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre; "> </span>pub_date__gte=datetime(2005,1,1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Todos los que empiezan por What entre 1/1/2005 y ahora.</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Cada filtro crea una consulta única</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">q1=Entry.objects.filter(headline__startswith=’What’)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">q2=q1.exclude(pub_date__gte=datetime.now())</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">q3=q2.filter(pub_date__gte=datetime(2005,1,1))</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Buscar un solo objeto con get()</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">one_entry=Entry.objects.get(pk=1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Si no hay datos salta la excepción DoesNotExist</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br></div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">from django.core.exceptions import ObjectdoesNotExist</div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">try:</div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">   one_entry=Entry.object.get(pk=numero)</div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">except ObjectDoesNotExist, e:</div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">   mensaje=("La entrada %n no existe" % (numero))</div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">
<br></div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">
<br></div><meta equiv="content-type" content="text/html; charset=utf-8"><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">
<br></div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">
<br></div><div style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; background-color: transparent; ">
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">En cambio filter()[0], no hace saltar ninguna excepción.</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Limitar el número de registros devueltos</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.all()[:5]  # los cinco primeros</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.all()[5:10]  # del quinto al décimo</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Buscar sobre campos</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Básicos: Son de la forma campo__tipobusqueda=valor</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Ejemplo: Entry.objects.filter(pub_date___lte=’2006-01-01’) se transforma en select from blog_entry where pub_date&lt;=’2006-01-01’</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">-&gt; exact : headline__exact=’algo’</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">-&gt; iexact: case insentive exact</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">-&gt; contains</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">-&gt; startswith</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">-&gt; endswith</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Relacionales</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.filter(blog__name__exact=’Pep’)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Blogs.objects.filter(entry__headline__contains=’Pep’, entry__pub_date__year=2006) </span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Todos los blogs que tengan alguna entrada cuyo titulo tenga Pep y se haya publicado en 2006</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Blogs.objects.filter(entry__headline__contains=’Pep’).filter(entry__pub_date__year=2006) </span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Todos los que tengan Pep y todos los que se hayan publicado en 2006</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Filtros que referencian a otros campos del mismo modelo</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">from django.db.models import F</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.filter(n_coments__gt=F(‘n_pingbacks’))</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">gt: greather than</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">n_pingbacks: valor de otro campo del mismo modelo</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Primary key</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Blog.objects.get(pk=valor)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">.get(pk__in=[1,4,7])</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">.get(pk__gt=14)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Caching</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Esta consulta se realiza dos veces:</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">print [e.headline from p in queryset]</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">print [e.pub_date from p in queryset]</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Esta, sólo una vez (cacheo de resultados):</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">queryset=Entry.objects.all()</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">print [p.headline form p in queryset] &lt;- En esta se cachea</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">print [p.pub_date form p in queryset] &lt;- en esta su usa la caché</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Consultas complejas con Q</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Las palabras clave en filter, etc... son ANDs, si queremos algo más complejo, necesitamos Qs</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">django.db.models.Q</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Q(question__startswith=’Who’) | Q(question__startswith=’What’)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Q(question__startswith=’Who’) | ~Q(question__startswith=’What’)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Poll.objects.get( Q(question__startswith=’Who’), </span>
<br><p style="text-indent: 36pt; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Q(pub_date=date(2005,5,2)) | Q(pub_date=date(2005,5,6)) )</span></p><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Comparando objetos</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Para comparar dos objetos usamos el == estándar de python</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">una_entrada==otra_entrada</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">La comparación se realiza siempre usando la clave primaria</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Borrando objetos</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.filter(pub_date__year=2005).delete()</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Borra todos los elementos y los foreign key que le apuntan </span><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">en cascada</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b=Blogs.objects.get(pk=1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b.delete()  -&gt; borra la entrada y todos sus comentarios</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Update de varios elementos</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Entry.objects.filter().update(headline=’Cambiado’)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><h4 style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: medium; "><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: bold; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Objetos relacionados</span></h4><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Si un modelo tiene un foreign key, podemos acceder al objeto foráneo via simple atributo del modelo:</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">e=Blog.objects.get(id=1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">e.entry_set.all() --&gt; todas las entradas del primer blog</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">e.entry_set.filter(headline__contains=’Pep’)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Si se ha usado el related_name en la definición del modelo, entonces ese es el nombre del atributo para acceder</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">blog=ForeignKey(Blog, related_name=’entries’)</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b=Blog.objects.get(id=1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b.entries.all()</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b.entries.count()</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Métodos del Foreign Manager:</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">relacionado.add(ob1, obj2, …) Añade al objeto relacionado</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">relacionado.create(**kwargs)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">relacionado.remove(obj1, obj2, …)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">relacionado.clear()  -&gt; borra todos los objetos relacionados</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">O también:</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b=Blog.objects.get(id=1)</span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">b.entry_set=[e1, e2, …] &lt;- un objeto iterable</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; ">Hacer siempre el save del objeto principal para que permanente.</span>
<br><span style="font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent; font-size: 11pt; background-color: transparent;"></span>
<br><span style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap; "> </span></div>
<div style="clear: both;"></div>
</div>
